But the pool is closed and there is no communication between the waiters? When checking in, I asked the check-in attendant which floor the swimming pool was on, and he answered that it was the third floor. In the morning, I called the concierge and asked what time the swimming pool would open. The answer was nine o'clock. When I asked if the water depth was one meter two or one meter five, the answer was one meter two. No one mentioned that the pool was closed. If I had known I could have changed hotels, it would have been really disappointing.
The child happily held the swimming ring and went there, but the waiter on the third floor said that the swimming pool could not be used. I saw a bunch of annual passes on the registration book that could be used to enter the gym. Why was my hotel not allowed in? I got angry and insisted on going in to take a look. It turned out that the water in the pool was dry, so I couldn't say anything.
